Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this information provides meaningful additional information regarding the company&#8217;s liquidity. </span></div><div style="padding-left:72pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Percentage changes in revenues and bookings on a local currency basis. Financial results in local currency are calculated by restating current period activity into U.S. dollars using the comparable prior year period&#8217;s foreign currency exchange rates. This approach is used for all results where the functional currency is not the U.S. dollar. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding changes in its revenues and bookings that excludes the effect of fluctuations in foreign currency exchange rates facilitates meaningful comparison of its revenues. </span></div><div style="padding-left:72pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Diluted earnings per share, effective tax rate, income before income taxes, income tax expense, and net income excluding gains on an investment. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding the effect of the investment gains facilitates an understanding as to the impacts of the investment and the company&#8217;s financial performance.</span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Reconciliations of these non-GAAP financial measures to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP are included in the news release. While Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this non-GAAP financial information is useful in evaluating Accenture&#8217;s operations, this information should be considered as supplemental in nature and not as a substitute for the related financial information prepared in accordance with GAAP.</span></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><span operating margin expands 10 basis points to 14.7%&#59; EPS increase 18% to $2.60 --</font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">-- For full fiscal year, revenues are $61.6 billion, a record increase of 22% in U.S. dollars and 26% in local currency&#59; operating margin expands 10 basis points to 15.2 --</font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">-- For full fiscal year, EPS are $10.71, a 17% increase from $9.16 for fiscal 2021 and a 22% increase from adjusted fiscal 2021 EPS of $8.80, which excluded $0.36 in gains on an investment --</font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">-- Free cash flow is $3.6 billion for fourth quarter and a record $8.8 billion for full year --</font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">-- New bookings are $18.4&#160;billion for fourth quarter and a record $71.7&#160;billion for full year, a 21% increase in U.S. dollars and 25% increase in local currency over full-year fiscal 2021 new bookings --</font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">-- 15% increase in quarterly dividend to $1.12 per share&#59; Board of Directors approves $3.0 billion of additional share repurchase authority --</font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">-- For fiscal year 2023, Accenture expects revenue growth of 8% to 11% in local currency and diluted EPS of $11.09 to $11.41 --</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">NEW YORK&#59; Sept. 22, 2022 &#8212; Accenture (NYSE&#58; ACN) reported financial results for the fourth quarter and full fiscal year ended Aug. 31, 2022. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">For the fourth quarter</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">, revenues were $15.4&#160;billion, an increase of 15% in U.S. dollars and 22.4% in local currency compared with the fourth quarter of fiscal 2021.&#160;Diluted earnings per share were $2.60, an 18% increase from $2.20 last year. Operating margin for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022 was 14.7%, an expansion of 10 basis points from the fourth quarter of fiscal 2021. Operating cash flow was $3.8&#160;billion and free cash flow was $3.6 billion. New bookings were $18.4&#160;billion.   </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">For the full fiscal year</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">, revenues were $61.6&#160;billion, a record increase of 22% in U.S. dollars and 26% in local currency compared with fiscal 2021. Diluted earnings per share increased 17% to $10.71 from $9.16 last year, which included gains on an investment of $0.36. Excluding these pre-tax gains, EPS increased 22% from adjusted EPS of $8.80 in fiscal 2021. Operating margin for fiscal 2022 was 15.2%, an expansion of 10 basis points. Operating cash flow for fiscal 2022 was $9.5 billion and free cash flow was a record $8.8&#160;billion. New bookings were a record $71.7&#160;billion.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Julie Sweet, chair and CEO, Accenture, said, &#8220;Our exceptional performance in fiscal 2022 is a testament to our ability to create enduring 360&#176; Value for all our stakeholders&#58; clients, people, shareholders, partners and communities. The depth, breadth and relevance of our services uniquely position us to help our clients achieve resilience, agility and growth across every part of the enterprise. Records across all financial metrics - new bookings, revenues, EPS and cash flow, reflect the continued successful execution of our growth strategy. We delivered these results while proudly making progress on our sustainability goals, including advancing inclusion and diversity&#59; exceeding 85% renewable electricity use in our offices and centers globally&#59; and continuing to make a positive impact on the communities where we work and live. I want to </font></div><div style="height:36pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:58.5pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">thank our 721,000 incredibly</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:115%"> </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">talented people, whose dedication and passion make us a trusted partner to our clients as we help them embrace today&#8217;s accelerated pace of change.&#8221; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Financial Review</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Fourth Quarter Fiscal 2022</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022 were $15.4 billion, compared with $13.4&#160;billion for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2021, an increase of 15% in U.S. dollars and 22.4% in local currency and at the upper end of the company&#8217;s guided range of $15.0 billion to $15.5 billion. The foreign-exchange impact for the quarter was approximately negative 7.5%, compared with the assumption of a negative 8% impact provided in the company&#8217;s third-quarter earnings release.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Wingdings',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.25pt">Consulting revenues were $8.33&#160;billion, an increase of 14% in U.S. dollars and 22% in local currency compared with the fourth quarter of fiscal 2021.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Wingdings',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.25pt">Outsourcing revenues were $7.09 billion, an increase of 16% in U.S. dollars and 23% in local currency compared with the fourth quarter of fiscal 2021.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Diluted EPS for the fourth quarter were $2.60, an increase of $0.40 or 18% from $2.20 for the fourth quarter last year. The $0.40 increase in EPS reflects&#58; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.15pt">a $0.36 increase from higher revenue and operating results&#59; </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.15pt">a $0.02 increase from lower non-operating expense&#59;</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.15pt">a $0.02 increase from a lower share count&#59; and </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.15pt">a $0.01 increase from a lower effective tax rate&#59;   </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">partially offset by</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Wingdings',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.25pt">a $0.01 decrease from higher non-controlling interests.   </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Gross margin (gross profit as a percentage of revenues) for the fourth quarter was 32.1%, compared with 33.3% for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2021. Selling, general and administrative (SG&#38;A) expenses for the fourth quarter were $2.68&#160;billion, or 17.4% of revenues, compared with $2.51&#160;billion, or 18.7% of revenues, for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2021. </font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Operating income for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022 was $2.27&#160;billion, or 14.7% of revenues, compared with $1.96 billion, or 14.6% of revenues, for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2021. Operating margin for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022 expanded 10 basis points.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The company&#8217;s effective tax rate for the fourth quarter was 24.6%, compared with 25.0% for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2021. Net income for the quarter was $1.69 billion, compared with $1.44&#160;billion for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2021. Operating cash flow for the fourth quarter was $3.79&#160;billion, and property and equipment additions were $177&#160;million. Free cash flow, defined as operating cash flow net of property and equipment additions, was $3.61&#160;billion. For the same period of fiscal 2021, operating cash flow was $2.44&#160;billion, property and equipment additions were $236&#160;million, and free cash flow was $2.20&#160;billion.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Days services outstanding, or DSOs, were 43 days at Aug. 31, 2022, compared with 38 days at Aug. 31, 2021. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture&#8217;s total cash balance at Aug. 31, 2022 was $7.9&#160;billion, compared with $8.2&#160;billion at Aug. 31, 2021.</font></div><div style="height:36pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div 31% in local currency from the fourth quarter last year.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font </font></div><div style="padding-left:18pt"><font><br></font></div><div><font </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font
